		   NULL, "\"In any case, we're in the boonies out here.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "迷信なんかが平気で幅を利かせてるんです。",
		   NULL, " It's kind of expected that there'd be some superstitions around.", Line_WaitForInput);


//なっはっはっはっは＠　東京から来られた赤坂さんには、ちょっと想像も付かないでしょうがねぇ。＠
	OutputLine(NULL, "なっはっはっはっは！",
		   NULL, " Na ha ha ha ha!", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　東京から来られた赤坂さんには、ちょっと想像も付かないでしょうがねぇ。」",
		   NULL, " Somebody from Tokyo like you, Akasaka-san, probably couldn't even begin to imagine it, could you?\"", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);


//　……人食い鬼が、自分たちの村を侵した代償として、大臣の孫をさらい、…食い殺した＠
	OutputLine(NULL, "　……人食い鬼が、自分たちの村を侵した代償として、大臣の孫をさらい、…食い殺した。",
		   NULL, "...The man-eating demons, as the price for violating the sanctity of their village, kidnapped the minister's grandson... and swallowed him whole.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);


//　そんな突拍子もない考えが浮かぶ￥
	OutputLine(NULL, "　そんな突拍子もない考えが浮かぶ。",
		   NULL, "That ludicrous idea flew through my head.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();


//　…あまりの下らない想像に、自分でも半ば呆れてしまう＠
	OutputLine(NULL, "　…あまりの下らない想像に、自分でも半ば呆れてしまう。",
		   NULL, "...It was so absurd, I was half-disgusted with myself.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);


//　大石氏にからかわれただけだ＠
	OutputLine(NULL, "　大石氏にからかわれただけだ。",
		   NULL, "Ooishi was just teasing me.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);


//　…下らない＠本当に下らない￥
	OutputLine(NULL, "　…下らない。",
		   NULL, "...Stupid.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "本当に下らない。",
		   NULL, " It was all really so stupid.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();


//　………思えば、私はもうこの時に、この怪しげな村の呪縛に囚われていたのかもしれない＠
	OutputLine(NULL, "　………思えば、私はもうこの時に、この怪しげな村の呪縛に囚われていたのかもしれない。",
		   NULL, "...Come to think of it, by then, I may have already been seized by the curse of that dubious village.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);


//　…それに気付くのには、……もう少しの時間が必要だった…￥
	OutputLine(NULL, "　…それに気付くのには、……もう少しの時間が必要だった…。",
		   NULL, "...For me to realize that... would take a little more time..", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();
